  Quantum AC Training  ·  IRS-assisted RSMA Satellite Comm.  ·  QC backend: GPU (CuPy)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

SystemConfig
  Topology  : K=5 users (fixed), M=1 IRS, N=24 elements/IRS
  Power     : P_S=50.0 dBm (100.00 W)
  Frequency : 1.58 GHz,  satellite alt=800.0 km
  Noise     : N(-30.0,10.0) dBW per-step  →  nominal σ²=1.00e-03 W
  Phase     : 2-bit → levels=[0.     1.5708 3.1416 4.7124] rad
  CSI error : multiplicative κ=0.05  (Δg = κ|g|ε, ε~CN(0,1))
  QoS/Demand: D_k=0.1 bps/Hz (R_tot ≥ D_k), λ_D=1.5, ε=0.001
  Geometry  : LoS radius=0.2 km, h_IRS=20 m (IRS on building rooftop)
  Mobility  : speed=1.5 m/s, dt=1.0 s (1.5 m/step)
  Blocking  : β_block=0.1, β_IRS=1.0, r_block=20 m
  Path loss : IRS→user exponent=3.5, d0=10 m

  Actor Pipeline  (4 stages per step)
  ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    1. Quantum IRS selection
       State  : a_t ∈ R^17  =  5×(1+2)+2×1  (affinity ‖ D_k ‖ |g_SU|)
       Encoder: 17 → B2-DualAE → 16  (z_t)  [IRS:2D + User:2×5D→P]
       Decoder: 16 → 64 → 128 → 17  (AE regulariser)
       QC     : 16-dim → 8 qubits (H+U_enc+U_var×3+1×CZ-bridge) → 22-dim+1×ZZ-cross(B4)  (o_hat)
       Post-NN: 38 → 256 → 128 → 5×2 logits
       Output : φ ∈ {0,…,1}^5  (2^5 combinations)
    2. PhaseMLP  (IRS phase shifts — active IRS only)
       State  : c^SRU_m ∈ R^31 per active IRS  ([Re+Im c^SRU(10) ‖ z_t(16) ‖ phi_mask(5)])
       Net    : 31 → 64 → 128 → 256 → 128 → 96  (shared weights, N=24 elements/IRS, categorical)
       Output : phase_idx ∈ {0..3}^{G×24}  (G ≤ 1 active IRS, expanded to 1×24)
    3. PowerMLP  (power allocation)
       State  : h_eff+z_t ∈ R^26  ([Re+Im h_eff(10) ‖ z_t(16)])
       Net    : 26 → 128 → 128 → 64 → 9  softmax → ×P_S
       Output : w_c_vec ∈ R^{G+1}  (per-group common, G≤1),  w_p ∈ R^5  (private)  [Σ=P_S]
    4. CkMLP  (common-rate split)
       State  : [D_k, R_p_k, R_c_g_k, shortfall_k, phi_k] ∈ R^25  (per user)
       Net    : 25 → 128 → 128 → 64 → 32 → 5  within-group softmax → C_k
       Output : C_k ∈ R^5  (Σ_{k∈g} C_k = R_c_g per group)

  Critic  (State-Value MLP  V(s))
    Input        : s_t (17)  =  17 total
    Architecture : 17 → 512 → 256 → 128 → 64 → 1  (V)

  Training plan
    Episodes       : 6000
    Steps/episode  : 200
    PPO epochs     : 6  (ε=0.2,  batch=64)
    Total steps    : 1,200,000
    γ (discount)   : 0.95
    AE loss weight : 0.5
    β entropy      : 0.001 → 0.0003  (anneal to 10% of training)
    LR schedule    : warm-up 20% eps, then linear decay to ×0.25
    GAE lambda (λ) : 0.9
    AE pretrain    : 5000 steps @ lr=0.001
    Data reupload  : True
    lr  ω/λθ/ξ/ψ  : 0.0001/0.0001/0.0003/0.0003
    Shots (train)  : 1500
    Seed           : 0

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  QC gradient : SPSA  n_reps=16  eps=0.1  (2048 circuits/update,  4x vs param-shift)
  Rollout buf : 12 ep x 200 steps = 2400 transitions/PPO call
